       <article class="post-8573 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-indie category-multiplayer category-retro category-stealth tag-contact-cowboy tag-contact-cowboy-game tag-indie-game tag-jupiter_hadley tag-ludum tag-ludum-dare-31 tag-pixel-art" id="post-8573">
        <header class="entry-header">
         <h1 class="entry-title">
          Contact Cowboy  Game Jam Build
         </h1>
         <div class="entry-meta">
          Posted on
          <a href="http://www.alphabetagamer.com/contact-cowboy-game-jam-build/" rel="bookmark" title="7:41 pm">
           <time class="entry-date updated" datetime="2014-12-13T19:41:15+00:00">
            December 13, 2014
           </time>
          </a>
          <span class="byline">
           by
           <span class="author vcard">
            <a class="url fn n" href="http://www.alphabetagamer.com/author/jupiter-hadley/" rel="author" title="View all posts by Jupiter Hadley">
             Jupiter Hadley
            </a>
           </span>
          </span>
         </div>
        </header>
        <div class="entry-content">
         <p>
          <a href="http://www.alphabetagamer.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/12/Contact-Cowboy.gif">
           <img alt="Contact Cowboy" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-8665" height="366" src="http://www.alphabetagamer.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/12/Contact-Cowboy.gif" width="650"/>
          </a>
         </p>
         <p>
          <em>
           Contact Cowboy
          </em>
          is a two player local multiplayer game made for the Ludum Dare 31. This game puts each of the players into a role. One player is a gunman, a person who has a gun and 6 bullets. Their objective is to kill the knife man so that he is unable to complete his objectives without wasting too many bullets. The knife man must grab C4 from the middle of the screen and plant it on a statue. Once that is done, he must go back and kill the gun man. If the gunman kills the wrong person or hits more than just the knifeman, then he loses. If the knifeman kills the wrong person, he also will lose.
         </p>
         <p>
          This game is not as easy as it seems. Each time you play it, you will appear as a new person, in a crowd of lots of people. It takes a minute to figure out who you are, let alone start completing your objectives. You must bluff, hope that your friend is not smart enough to find out who you are and kill you. This game is simple, but the graphics andgameplay very well done.
          <span style="color: #444444;">
           Its a clever local multiplayer
          </span>
          battle of wits
          <span style="color: #444444;">
           that sees you trying to outsmart your friends, then kill them.
          </span>
         </p>
         <p>
          Play Contact Cowboy inyour browser
          <a href="//ludumdare.com/compo/ludum-dare-31/?action=preview&amp;uid=35879" target="_blank">
           HERE
          </a>
          <br/>
          <script>
           google_ad_client="ca-pub-7383502787775729";google_ad_slot="5369699040";google_ad_width=728;google_ad_height=90;
          </script>
          <br/>
          <script src="//pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/show_ads.js">
           /*&lt;![CDATA[*/&lt;p&gt;/*]]&gt;*/
          </script>
         </p>
